9th - 32nd Decklists
====================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX GUANGZHOU 2016](/en/events/coverage/gpgua16)
 on August 28, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











Since *Eldritch Moon* just got added into the mix, you guys must be curious about how that has impacted the Modern metagame. Here are the top performing decklists of the weekend, with most of these pilots only a win or two away from the Top 8!







#### Joe Soh's B/R Eldrazi - 9th


##### 
 Grand Prix Guangzhou 2016






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
